default.\n\tEvaluationInterval model.Duration `yaml:\"evaluation_interval,omitempty\"`\n\t// Offset the rule evaluation timestamp of this particular group by the specified duration into the past to `yaml:\"query_log_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// File to which scrape failures are logged.\n\tScrapeFailureLogFile string `yaml:\"scrape_failure_log_file,omitempty\"`\n\t// The labels to add to any timeseries that this Prometheus instance scrapes.\n\tExternalLabels labels.Labels `yaml:\"external_labels,omitempty\"`\n\t// An uncompressed response body larger than this many bytes will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tBodySizeLimit units.Base2Bytes `yaml:\"body_size_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many samples post metric-relabeling will cause the scrape to\n\t// fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tSampleLimit uint `yaml:\"sample_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many targets after the target relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrapes to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tTargetLimit uint `yaml:\"target_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many labels post metric-relabeling will cause the scrape to\n\t// fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelLimit uint `yaml:\"label_name_length_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this label value length post metric-relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelValueLengthLimit uint `yaml:\"label_value_length_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// Keep no more than this many dropped targets per job.\n\t// 0 means no limit.\n\tKeepDroppedTargets uint `yaml:\"keep_dropped_targets,omitempty\"`\n\t// Allow UTF8 Metric and Label Names. Can be blank in config files but must\n\t// have a value if a GlobalConfig is created programmatically.\n\tMetricNameValidationScheme model.ValidationScheme `yaml:\"metric_name_validation_scheme,omitempty\"`\n\t// Metric name escaping mode to request through content negotiation. Can be\n\t// blank in config files but must have a value if a ScrapeConfig is created\n\t// programmatically.\n\tMetricNameEscapingScheme string `yaml:\"metric_name_escaping_scheme,omitempty\"`\n\t// protocol for scraping metrics.\ntype ScrapeProtocol string\n\n// Validate returns error if given scrape protocol is not supported.\nfunc (s ScrapeProtocol) Validate() error {\n\tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape protocol %v, supported: %v\",\n\t\t\ts, func() (ret []string) {\n\t\t\t\tfor k := range ScrapeProtocolsHeaders {\n\t\t\t\t\tret = append(ret, string(k))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tsort.Strings(ret)\n\t\t\t\treturn ret\n\t\t\t}())\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// HeaderMediaType returns the MIME mediaType for a particular ScrapeProtocol.\nfunc (s ScrapeProtocol) HeaderMediaType() string {\n\tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\tmediaType, _, err := mime.ParseMediaType(ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\treturn mediaType\n}\n\nvar (\n\tPrometheusProto      ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusProto\"\n\tPrometheusText0_0_4  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText0.0.4\"\n\tPrometheusText1_0_0  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText1.0.0\"\n\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText0.0.1\"\n\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText1.0.0\"\n\tUTF8NamesHeader      string         = model.EscapingKey + \"=\" + model.AllowUTF8\n\n\tScrapeProtocolsHeaders = map[ScrapeProtocol]string{\n\t\tPrometheusProto:      \"application/vnd.google.protobuf;proto=io.prometheus.client.MetricFamily;encoding=delimited\",\n\t\tPrometheusText0_0_4:  \"text/plain;version=0.0.4\",\n\t\tPrometheusText1_0_0:  \"text/plain;version=1.0.0\",\n\t\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1: \"application/openmetrics-text;version=0.0.1\",\n\t\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0: \"application/openmetrics-text;version=1.0.0\",\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultScrapeProtocols is the set of scrape protocols that will be proposed\n\t// to scrape target, ordered by priority.\n\tDefaultScrapeProtocols = []ScrapeProtocol{\n\t\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0,\n\t\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1,\n\t\tPrometheusText1_0_0,\n\t\tPrometheusText0_0_4,\n\t}\n\n\t// DefaultProtoFirstScrapeProtocols is like DefaultScrapeProtocols, but it\n\t// favors protobuf Prometheus exposition format.\n\t// Used by default by the \"scrape_native_histograms\" option and for certain\n\t// feature-flags like \"created-timestamp-zero-ingestion\".\n\tDefaultProtoFirstScrapeProtocols = []ScrapeProtocol{\n\t\tPrometheusProto,\n\t\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0,\n\t\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1,\n\t\tPrometheusText1_0_0,\n\t\tPrometheusText0_0_4,\n\t}\n)\n\n// validateAcceptScrapeProtocols return errors if we see problems with accept scrape protocols option.\nfunc validateAcceptScrapeProtocols(sps []ScrapeProtocol) error {\n\tif len(sps) == 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"scrape_protocols cannot be empty\")\n\t}\n\tdups := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, sp := range sps {\n\t\tif _, ok := dups[strings.ToLower(string(sp))]; ok {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"duplicated protocol in scrape_protocols, got %v\", sps)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err := sp.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"scrape_protocols: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tdups[strings.ToLower(string(sp))] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\nfunc (c *GlobalConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tc.QueryLogFile = config.JoinDir(dir, c.QueryLogFile)\n\tc.ScrapeFailureLogFile = config.JoinDir(dir, c.ScrapeFailureLogFile)\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\nfunc (c *GlobalConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error {\n\t// Create a clean global config as the previous one was already populated\n\t// by the default due to the YAML parser behavior for empty blocks.\n\tgc := &GlobalConfig{}\n\ttype plain GlobalConfig\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(gc)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tswitch gc.MetricNameValidationScheme {\n\tcase model.UTF8Validation, model.LegacyValidation:\n\tdefault:\n\t\tgc.MetricNameValidationScheme = DefaultGlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme\n\t}\n\n\tif err := gc.ExternalLabels.Validate(func(l !model.LabelValue(l.Value).IsValid() {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%q is not a valid label value\", l.Value)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// First set the correct scrape interval, then check that the timeout\n\t// (inferred or explicit) is not greater than that.\n\tif gc.ScrapeInterval == 0 {\n\t\tgc.ScrapeInterval = DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeInterval\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeTimeout > gc.ScrapeInterval {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"global scrape timeout greater than scrape interval\")\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeTimeout == 0 {\n\t\tgc.ScrapeTimeout = min(DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeTimeout, gc.ScrapeInterval)\n\t}\n\tif gc.EvaluationInterval == 0 {\n\t\tgc.EvaluationInterval = DefaultGlobalConfig.EvaluationInterval\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeNativeHistograms == nil {\n\t\tgc.ScrapeNativeHistograms = DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeNativeHistograms\n\t}\n\tif gc.ExtraScrapeMetrics == nil {\n\t\tgc.ExtraScrapeMetrics = DefaultGlobalConfig.ExtraScrapeMetrics\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeProtocols == nil {\n\t\tif DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeProtocols != nil {\n\t\t\t// This is the case where the defaults are set due to a feature flag.\n\t\t\t// E.g. if the created-timestamp-zero-ingestion feature flag is\n\t\t\t// used.\n\t\t\tgc.ScrapeProtocols = DefaultGlobalConfig.ScrapeProtocols\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Otherwise, we leave ScrapeProtocols at nil for now. In the\n\t\t// per-job scrape config, we have to recognize the unset case to\n\t\t// correctly set the default depending on the local value of\n\t\t// ScrapeNativeHistograms.\n\t}\n\tif gc.ScrapeProtocols != nil {\n\t\t// Only validate if not-nil at this point.\n\t\tif err := validateAcceptScrapeProtocols(gc.ScrapeProtocols); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%w for global config\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t*c = *gc\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// isZero returns true iff the global config is the zero value.\nfunc (c *GlobalConfig) isZero() bool {\n\treturn c.ExternalLabels.IsEmpty() &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeInterval == 0 &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeTimeout == 0 &&\n\t\tc.EvaluationInterval == 0 &&\n\t\tc.RuleQueryOffset == 0 &&\n\t\tc.QueryLogFile == \"\" &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeFailureLogFile == \"\" &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeProtocols == nil &&\n\t\tc.ScrapeNativeHistograms == nil &&\n\t\t!c.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB &&\n\t\t!c.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms &&\n\t\tc.BodySizeLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.SampleLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.TargetLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.LabelLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.LabelNameLengthLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.LabelValueLengthLimit == 0 &&\n\t\tc.KeepDroppedTargets == 0 &&\n\t\tc.MetricNameValidationScheme == model.UnsetValidation &&\n\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme == \"\" &&\n\t\tc.ExtraScrapeMetrics == nil\n}\n\nconst DefaultGoGCPercentage = 75\n\n// RuntimeConfig configures the values for the process behavior.\ntype RuntimeConfig struct {\n\t// The Go garbage collection target percentage.\n\tGoGC int `yaml:\"gogc,omitempty\"`\n\n\t// Below are guidelines for adding a new field:\n\t//\n\t// For config that shouldn't change after startup, you might want to use\n\t// flags https://prometheus.io/docs/prometheus/latest/command-line/prometheus/.\n\t//\n\t// Consider when the new field is first applied: at the very beginning of instance\n\t// startup, after the TSDB is loaded etc. See https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/pull/16491\n\t// for an example.\n\t//\n\t// Provide a test covering various scenarios: empty config file, empty or incomplete runtime\n\t// config block, precedence over other inputs (e.g., env vars, if applicable) etc.\n\t// See TestRuntimeGOGCConfig (or https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/pull/15238).\n\t// The test should also verify behavior on reloads, since this config should be\n\t// adjustable at runtime.\n}\n\n// isZero returns true iff the global config is the zero value.\nfunc (c *RuntimeConfig) isZero() bool {\n\treturn c.GoGC == 0\n}\n\ntype ScrapeConfigs struct {\n\tScrapeConfigs []*ScrapeConfig `yaml:\"scrape_configs,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// ScrapeConfig configures a scraping unit for Prometheus.\ntype ScrapeConfig struct {\n\t// The job name to which the job label is set by default.\n\tJobName string `yaml:\"job_name\"`\n\t// Indicator whether the scraped metrics should remain unmodified.\n\tHonorLabels bool `yaml:\"honor_labels,omitempty\"`\n\t// Indicator whether the scraped timestamps should be respected.\n\tHonorTimestamps bool `yaml:\"honor_timestamps\"`\n\t// the\n\t// scrapes to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tTargetLimit uint `yaml:\"target_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this many labels post metric-relabeling will cause the scrape to\n\t// fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelLimit uint `yaml:\"label_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this label name length post metric-relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no limit.\n\tLabelNameLengthLimit uint `yaml:\"label_name_length_limit,omitempty\"`\n\t// More than this label value length post metric-relabeling will cause the\n\t// scrape to fail. 0 means no increase the factor sufficiently.\n\tNativeHistogramMinBucketFactor float64 `yaml:\"native_histogram_min_bucket_factor,omitempty\"`\n\t// Keep no more than this many dropped targets per job.\n\t// 0 Whether to enable additional scrape metrics.\n\t// When enabled, Prometheus stores samples for scrape_timeout_seconds,\n\t// scrape_sample_limit, and scrape_body_size_bytes.\n\t// If not set (nil), `yaml:\",inline\"`\n\n\t// List of target relabel configurations.\n\tRelabelConfigs []*relabel.Config `yaml:\"relabel_configs,omitempty\"`\n\t// List of metric relabel configurations.\n\tMetricRelabelConfigs []*relabel.Config `yaml:\"metric_relabel_configs,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) SetDirectory(dir string) {\n\tc.ServiceDiscoveryConfigs.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.HTTPClientConfig.SetDirectory(dir)\n\tc.ScrapeFailureLogFile = config.JoinDir(dir, c.ScrapeFailureLogFile)\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error {\n\t*c = DefaultScrapeConfig\n\tif err := discovery.UnmarshalYAMLWithInlineConfigs(c, unmarshal); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tif len(c.JobName) == 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"job_name is empty\")\n\t}\n\n\t// The UnmarshalYAML method of HTTPClientConfig is not being called because it's not a pointer.\n\t// We cannot make it a pointer as the parser panics for inlined pointer structs.\n\t// Thus we just do its validation here.\n\tif err := c.HTTPClientConfig.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// Check for users putting URLs in target groups.\n\tif len(c.RelabelConfigs) == 0 {\n\t\tif err := checkStaticTargets(c.ServiceDiscoveryConfigs); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, rlcfg := range c.RelabelConfigs {\n\t\tif rlcfg == nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null target relabeling rule in scrape config\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, rlcfg := range c.MetricRelabelConfigs {\n\t\tif rlcfg == nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null metric relabeling rule in scrape config\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Validate validates scrape config, but also fills relevant default values from global config if needed.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) Validate(globalConfig GlobalConfig) error {\n\tif c == nil {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null scrape config section\")\n\t}\n\t// First set the correct scrape interval, then check that the timeout\n\t// (inferred or explicit) is not greater than that.\n\tif c.ScrapeInterval == 0 {\n\t\tc.ScrapeInterval = globalConfig.ScrapeInterval\n\t}\n\tif c.ScrapeTimeout > c.ScrapeInterval {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"scrape timeout greater than scrape interval for scrape config with job name %q\", c.JobName)\n\t}\n\tif c.ScrapeTimeout == 0 {\n\t\tc.ScrapeTimeout = min(globalConfig.ScrapeTimeout, c.ScrapeInterval)\n\t}\n\tif c.BodySizeLimit == 0 {\n\t\tc.BodySizeLimit = globalConfig.BodySizeLimit\n\t}\n\tif c.SampleLimit == 0 {\n\t\tc.SampleLimit = globalConfig.SampleLimit\n\t}\n\tif c.TargetLimit == 0 {\n\t\tc.TargetLimit = globalConfig.TargetLimit\n\t}\n\tif c.LabelLimit == 0 {\n\t\tc.LabelLimit = globalConfig.LabelLimit\n\t}\n\tif c.LabelNameLengthLimit == 0 {\n\t\tc.LabelNameLengthLimit = globalConfig.LabelNameLengthLimit\n\t}\n\tif c.LabelValueLengthLimit == 0 {\n\t\tc.LabelValueLengthLimit = globalConfig.LabelValueLengthLimit\n\t}\n\tif c.KeepDroppedTargets == 0 {\n\t\tc.KeepDroppedTargets = globalConfig.KeepDroppedTargets\n\t}\n\tif c.ScrapeFailureLogFile == \"\" {\n\t\tc.ScrapeFailureLogFile = globalConfig.ScrapeFailureLogFile\n\t}\n\tif c.ScrapeNativeHistograms == nil {\n\t\tc.ScrapeNativeHistograms = globalConfig.ScrapeNativeHistograms\n\t}\n\tif c.ExtraScrapeMetrics == nil {\n\t\tc.ExtraScrapeMetrics = globalConfig.ExtraScrapeMetrics\n\t}\n\n\tif c.ScrapeProtocols == nil {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase globalConfig.ScrapeProtocols != nil:\n\t\t\t// global ScrapeProtocols either set explicitly or via a\n\t\t\t// default triggered by a feature flag. This overrides\n\t\t\t// the selection based on locally active scraping of\n\t\t\t// native histograms.\n\t\t\tc.ScrapeProtocols = globalConfig.ScrapeProtocols\n\t\tcase c.ScrapeNativeHistogramsEnabled():\n\t\t\tc.ScrapeProtocols = DefaultProtoFirstScrapeProtocols\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tc.ScrapeProtocols = DefaultScrapeProtocols\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif err := validateAcceptScrapeProtocols(c.ScrapeProtocols); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%w for scrape config with job name %q\", err, c.JobName)\n\t}\n\n\tif c.ScrapeFallbackProtocol != \"\" {\n\t\tif err := c.ScrapeFallbackProtocol.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid fallback_scrape_protocol for scrape config with job name %q: %w\", c.JobName, err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t//nolint:staticcheck\n\tif model.NameValidationScheme != model.UTF8Validation {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"model.NameValidationScheme must be set to UTF8\")\n\t}\n\n\tswitch globalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme {\n\tcase model.LegacyValidation, model.UTF8Validation:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"global name validation method must be set\")\n\t}\n\t// Scrapeconfig validation scheme matches global if left blank.\n\tlocalValidationUnset := false\n\tswitch c.MetricNameValidationScheme {\n\tcase model.UnsetValidation:\n\t\tlocalValidationUnset = true\n\t\tc.MetricNameValidationScheme = globalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme\n\tcase model.LegacyValidation, model.UTF8Validation:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape config name validation method specified, must be either '', 'legacy' or 'utf8', got %s\", c.MetricNameValidationScheme)\n\t}\n\n\t// Escaping scheme is based on the validation scheme if left blank.\n\tswitch globalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme {\n\tcase \"\":\n\t\tif globalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme == model.LegacyValidation {\n\t\t\tglobalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.EscapeUnderscores\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tglobalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.AllowUTF8\n\t\t}\n\tcase model.AllowUTF8, model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown global name escaping method specified, must be one of '%s', '%s', '%s', or '%s', got %q\", model.AllowUTF8, model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues, globalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme)\n\t}\n\n\t// Similarly, if ScrapeConfig escaping scheme is blank, infer it from the\n\t// ScrapeConfig validation scheme if that was set, or the Global validation\n\t// scheme if the ScrapeConfig validation scheme was also not set. This ensures\n\t// that local ScrapeConfigs that only specify Legacy validation do not inherit\n\t// the global AllowUTF8 escaping setting, which is an error.\n\tif c.MetricNameEscapingScheme == \"\" {\n\t\t//nolint:gocritic\n\t\tif localValidationUnset {\n\t\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme = globalConfig.MetricNameEscapingScheme\n\t\t} else if c.MetricNameValidationScheme == model.LegacyValidation {\n\t\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.EscapeUnderscores\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tc.MetricNameEscapingScheme = model.AllowUTF8\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tswitch c.MetricNameEscapingScheme {\n\tcase model.AllowUTF8:\n\t\tif c.MetricNameValidationScheme != model.UTF8Validation {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"utf8 metric names requested but validation scheme is not set to UTF8\")\n\t\t}\n\tcase model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues:\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape config name escaping method specified, must be one of '%s', '%s', '%s', or '%s', got %q\", model.AllowUTF8, model.EscapeUnderscores, model.EscapeDots, model.EscapeValues, c.MetricNameEscapingScheme)\n\t}\n\n\tif c.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB == nil {\n\t\tglobal := globalConfig.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB\n\t\tc.ConvertClassicHistogramsToNHCB = &global\n\t}\n\n\tif c.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms == nil {\n\t\tglobal := globalConfig.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms\n\t\tc.AlwaysScrapeClassicHistograms = &global\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, rc := range c.RelabelConfigs {\n\t\tif err := rc.Validate(c.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, rc := range c.MetricRelabelConfigs {\n\t\tif err := rc.Validate(c.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// MarshalYAML implements the yaml.Marshaler interface.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) MarshalYAML() (any, error) {\n\treturn discovery.MarshalYAMLWithInlineConfigs(c)\n}\n\n// ToEscapingScheme wraps the equivalent common library function with the\n// desired default behavior based on the given validation scheme. This is a\n// workaround for third party exporters that don't set the escaping scheme.\nfunc ToEscapingScheme(s string, v model.ValidationScheme) (model.EscapingScheme, error) {\n\tif s == \"\" {\n\t\tswitch v {\n\t\tcase model.UTF8Validation:\n\t\t\treturn model.NoEscaping, nil\n\t\tcase model.LegacyValidation:\n\t\t\treturn model.UnderscoreEscaping, nil\n\t\tcase model.UnsetValidation:\n\t\t\treturn model.NoEscaping, fmt.Errorf(\"ValidationScheme is unset: %s\", v)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"unhandled validation scheme: %s\", v))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn model.ToEscapingScheme(s)\n}\n\n// ScrapeNativeHistogramsEnabled returns whether to scrape native histograms.\nfunc (c *ScrapeConfig) ScrapeNativeHistogramsEnabled() bool 227→\t\t}))\n   228→\n   229→\treturn &Client{\n   230→\t\tremoteName:       name,\n   231→\t\turlString:        conf.URL.String(),\n   232→\t\tClient:           httpClient,\n   233→\t\tretryOnRateLimit: conf.RetryOnRateLimit,\n   234→\t\ttimeout:          time.Duration(conf.Timeout),\n   235→\t\twriteProtoMsg:    writeProtoMsg,\n   236→\t\twriteCompression: remoteapi.SnappyBlockCompression,\n   237→\t}, nil\n   238→}\n   239→\n   240→func newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(h map[string]string, underlyingRT http.RoundTripper) *injectHeadersRoundTripper {\n   241→\treturn &injectHeadersRoundTripper{headers: h, RoundTripper: underlyingRT}\n   242→}\n   243→\n   244→type injectHeadersRoundTripper struct {\n   245→\theaders map[string]string\n   246→\thttp.RoundTripper\n   247→}\n   248→\n   249→func (t *injectHeadersRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n   250→\tfor key, value := range t.headers {\n   251→\t\treq.Header.Set(key, value)\n   252→\t}\n   253→\treturn t.RoundTripper.RoundTrip(req)\n   254→}\n   255→\n   256→const defaultBackoff = 0\n   257→\n   258→type RecoverableError struct {\n   259→\terror\n   260→\tretryAfter model.Duration\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→// Store sends a batch of samples to the HTTP endpoint, the request is the proto marshalled\n   264→// and encoded bytes from codec.go.\n   265→func (c *Client) Store(ctx context.Context, req []byte, attempt int) (WriteResponseStats, error) {\n   266→\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(req))\n   267→\tif err != nil {\n   268→\t\t// Errors from NewRequest are from unparsable URLs, so are not\n   269→\t\t// recoverable.\n   270→\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, err\n   271→\t}\n   272→\n   273→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", string(c.writeCompression))\n   274→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", remoteWriteContentTypeHeaders[c.writeProtoMsg])\n   275→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n   276→\tif c.writeProtoMsg == remoteapi.WriteV1MessageType {\n   277→\t\t// Compatibility mode for 1.0.\n   278→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion1HeaderValue)\n   279→\t} else {\n   280→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion20HeaderValue)\n   281→\t}\n   282→\n   283→\tif attempt > 0 {\n   284→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Retry-Attempt\", strconv.Itoa(attempt))\n   285→\t}\n   286→\n   287→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, c.timeout)\n   288→\tdefer cancel()\n   289→\n   290→\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Store\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n   291→\tdefer span.End()\n   292→\n   293→\thttpResp, err := c.Client.Do(httpReq.WithContext(ctx))\n   294→\tif err != nil {\n   295→\t\t// Errors from Client.Do are from (for example) network errors, so are\n   296→\t\t// recoverable.\n   297→\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, RecoverableError{err, defaultBackoff}\n   298→\t}\n   299→\tdefer func() {\n   300→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   301→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   302→\t}()\n   303→\n   304→\t// NOTE(bwplotka): Only PRW2 spec defines response HTTP headers. However, spec does not block\n   305→\t// PRW1 from sending them too for reliability. Support this case.\n   306→\t//\n   307→\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n   308→\t// Parsing error means there were some response header values we can't parse,\n   309→\t// we can continue handling.\n   310→\trs, _ := ParseWriteResponseStats(httpResp)\n   311→\n   312→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 2 {\n   313→\t\treturn rs, nil\n   314→\t}\n   315→\n   316→\t// Handling errors e.g. read potential error in the body.\n   317→\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n   318→\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(io.LimitReader(httpResp.Body, maxErrMsgLen))\n   319→\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"server returned HTTP status %s: %s\", httpResp.Status, body)\n   320→\n   321→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 5 ||\n   322→\t\t(c.retryOnRateLimit && httpResp.StatusCode == http.StatusTooManyRequests) {\n   323→\t\treturn rs, RecoverableError{err, retryAfterDuration(httpResp.Header.Get(\"Retry-After\"))}\n   324→\t}\n   325→\treturn rs, err\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// retryAfterDuration returns the duration for the Retry-After header. In case of any errors, it\n   329→// returns the defaultBackoff as if the header was never supplied.\n   330→func retryAfterDuration(t string) model.Duration {\n   331→\tparsedDuration, err := time.Parse(http.TimeFormat, t)\n   332→\tif err == nil {\n   333→\t\ts := time.Until(parsedDuration).Seconds()\n   334→\t\treturn model.Duration(s) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n   335→\t}\n   336→\t// The duration can be in seconds.\n   337→\td, err := strconv.Atoi(t)\n   338→\tif err != nil {\n   339→\t\treturn defaultBackoff\n   340→\t}\n   341→\treturn model.Duration(d) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// Name uniquely identifies the client.\n   345→func (c *Client) Name() string {\n   346→\treturn c.remoteName\n   347→}\n   348→\n   349→// Endpoint is the remote read or write endpoint.\n   350→func (c *Client) Endpoint() string {\n   351→\treturn c.urlString\n   352→}\n   353→\n   354→// Read reads from a remote endpoint. The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n   355→// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n   356→func (c *Client) Read(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   357→\treturn c.ReadMultiple(ctx, []*prompb.Query{query}, sortSeries)\n   358→}\n   359→\n   360→// ReadMultiple reads from a remote endpoint using multiple queries in a single request.\n   361→// The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n   362→// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n   363→// Returns a single SeriesSet with interleaved series from all queries.\n   364→func (c *Client) ReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   365→\tc.readQueries.Inc()\n   366→\tdefer c.readQueries.Dec()\n   367→\n   368→\treq := &prompb.ReadRequest{\n   369→\t\tQueries:               queries,\n   370→\t\tAcceptedResponseTypes: c.acceptedResponseTypes,\n   371→\t}\n   372→\n   373→\thttpResp, cancel, start, err := c.executeReadRequest(ctx, req)\n   374→\tif err != nil {\n   375→\t\treturn nil, for reading data.\n   382→func (c *Client) executeReadRequest(ctx context.Context, req *prompb.ReadRequest) (*http.Response, context.CancelFunc, time.Time, error) {\n   383→\tdata, err := proto.Marshal(req)\n   384→\tif err != nil {\n   385→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to marshal read request: %w\", err)\n   386→\t}\n   387→\n   388→\tcompressed := snappy.Encode(nil, data)\n   389→\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(compressed))\n   390→\tif err != nil {\n   391→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to create request: %w\", err)\n   392→\t}\n   393→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n   394→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Accept-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n   395→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/x-protobuf\")\n   396→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n   397→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"X-Prometheus-Remote-Read-Version\", \"0.1.0\")\n   398→\n   399→\terrTimeout := fmt.Errorf(\"%w: request timed out after %s\", context.DeadlineExceeded, c.timeout)\n   400→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeoutCause(ctx, c.timeout, errTimeout)\n   401→\n   402→\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Read\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n   403→\tdefer span.End()\n   404→\n   405→\tstart := time.Now()\n  410→\t}\n   411→\n   412→\treturn httpResp, cancel, start, nil\n   413→}\n   414→\n   415→// handleReadResponse processes the HTTP response and returns a SeriesSet.\n   416→func (c *Client) handleReadResponse(httpResp *http.Response, req *prompb.ReadRequest, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool, start time.Time, cancel context.CancelFunc) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   417→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n   418→\t\t// Make an attempt at getting an error message.\n   419→\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   420→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   421→\n   422→\t\tcancel()\n   423→\t\terrStr := strings.Trim(string(body), \"\\n\")\n   424→\t\terr := errors.New(errStr)\n   425→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"remote server %s returned http status %s: %w\", c.urlString, httpResp.Status, err)\n   426→\t}\n   427→\n   428→\tcontentType := httpResp.Header.Get(\"Content-Type\")\n   429→\n   430→\tswitch {\n   431→\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-protobuf\"):\n   432→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   433→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\", 438→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   439→\n   440→\t\ts := NewChunkedReader(httpResp.Body, c.chunkedReadLimit, nil)\n   441→\t\treturn 450→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   451→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\", strconv.Itoa(httpResp.StatusCode)).Inc()\n   452→\t\tcancel()\n   453→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported content type: %s\", contentType)\n   454→\t}\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→func (*Client) handleSampledResponse(req *prompb.ReadRequest, httpResp *http.Response, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   458→\tcompressed, err := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   459→\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response. HTTP status code: %s: %w\", httpResp.Status, err)\n   461→\t}\n   462→\tdefer func() {\n   463→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   464→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   465→\t}()\n   466→\n   467→\tuncompressed, err := snappy.Decode(nil, compressed)\n   468→\tif err != nil {\n   469→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response: %w\", err)\n   470→\t}\n   471→\n   472→\tvar resp prompb.ReadResponse\n   473→\terr = proto.Unmarshal(uncompressed, &resp)\n   474→\tif err != nil {\n   475→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to unmarshal response body: %w\", err)\n   476→\t}\n   477→\n   478→\tif len(resp.Results) != len(req.Queries) {\n   479→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"responses: want %d, got %d\", len(req.Queries), len(resp.Results))\n   480→\t}\n   481→\n   482→\treturn combineQueryResults(resp.Results, sortSeries)\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→// combineQueryResults combines multiple query results into a single SeriesSet,\n   486→// handling both sorted and unsorted cases appropriately.\n   487→func combineQueryResults(results []*prompb.QueryResult, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   488→\tif len(results) == 0 {\n   489→\t\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: nil, cur: 0}, nil\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\tif len(results) == 1 {\n   493→\t\treturn FromQueryResult(sortSeries, results[0]), nil\n   494→\t}\n   495→\n   496→\t// Multiple queries case - combine all results\n   497→\tif sortSeries {\n   498→\t\t// When sorting is requested, use MergeSeriesSet which can efficiently merge sorted inputs\n   499→\t\tvar allSeriesSets []storage.SeriesSet\n   500→\t\tfor _, result := range results {\n   501→\t\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   502→\t\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   503→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   504→\t\t\t}\n   505→\t\t\tallSeriesSets = append(allSeriesSets, seriesSet)\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\t\treturn storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(allSeriesSets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge), nil\n   508→\t}\n   509→\n   510→\t// When sorting is not requested, just concatenate all series without using MergeSeriesSet\n   511→\t// since MergeSeriesSet requires sorted inputs\n   512→\tvar allSeries []storage.Series\n   513→\tfor _, result := range results {\n   514→\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   515→\t\tfor seriesSet.Next() {\n   516→\t\t\tallSeries = append(allSeries, seriesSet.At())\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   519→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\t}\n   522→\n   523→\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: allSeries, cur: 0}, nil\n   524→}\n   525→\n   526→// handleChunkedResponseImpl handles chunked responses for both single and multiple queries.\n   527→func (*Client) handleChunkedResponseImpl(s *ChunkedReader, httpResp *http.Response, queries []*prompb.Query, onClose func(error)) storage.SeriesSet {\n   528→\t// For multiple queries in chunked response, we'll still use the existing infrastructure\n   529→\t// but we need to provide the timestamp range that covers all queries\n   530→\tvar minStartTs, maxEndTs int64 = math.MaxInt64, math.MinInt64\n   531→\n   532→\tfor _, query := range queries {\n   533→\t\tminStartTs = min(minStartTs, query.StartTimestampMs)\n   534→\t\tmaxEndTs = max(maxEndTs, query.EndTimestampMs)\n   535→\t}\n   536→\n   537→\treturn NewChunkedSeriesSet(s, httpResp.Body, minStartTs, maxEndTs, onClose)\n   538→}\n   539→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. necessary.\ntype ReadClient interface {\n\tRead(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error)\n\tReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error)\n}\n\n// NewReadClient creates a new client for remote read.\nfunc NewReadClient(name string, conf *ClientConfig, optFuncs ...config_util.HTTPClientOption) (ReadClient, error) {\n\thttpClient, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(conf.HTTPClientConfig, \"remote_storage_read_client\", optFuncs...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tt := remoteReadQueryDuration.MustCurryWith(prometheus.Labels{remoteName: name, endpoint: conf.URL.String()}),\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// NewWriteClient creates a new client for remote write.\nfunc NewWriteClient(name string, conf *ClientConfig) (WriteClient, error) {\n\tvar httpOpts []config_util.HTTPClientOption\n\tif conf.RoundRobinDNS {\n\t\thttpOpts = http.RoundTripper) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n   238→\tif next == nil {\n   239→\t\tnext = http.DefaultTransport\n   240→\t}\n   241→\n   242→\tcred, err := newTokenCredential(cfg)\n   243→\tif err != nil {\n   244→\t\treturn nil, err\n   245→\t}\n   246→\n   247→\ttokenProvider, err := newTokenProvider(cfg, cred)\n   248→\tif err != nil {\n   249→\t\treturn nil, err\n   250→\t}\n   251→\n This accessToken is attached to the Authorization header while making requests.\n   371→func newTokenProvider(cfg *AzureADConfig, cred azcore.TokenCredential) (*tokenProvider, error) {\n   372→\tvar {\n   395→\ttokenProvider.mu.Lock()\n   396→\tdefer tokenProvider.mu.Unlock()\n   397→\tif tokenProvider.valid() {\n   398→\t\treturn tokenProvider.token, nil\n   399→\t}\n   400→\terr := tokenProvider.getToken(ctx)\n   401→\tif err != nil {\n   402→\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Failed to get access token: \" + err.Error())\n   403→\t}\n   404→\treturn tokenProvider.token, nil\n   405→}\n   406→\n   407→// valid checks if the token in the token provider is valid and not expired.\n   408→func (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) valid() bool {\n   409→\tif len(tokenProvider.token) == 0 {\n   410→\t\treturn false\n   411→\t}\n   412→\tif tokenProvider.refreshTime.After(time.Now().UTC()) {\n   413→\t\treturn true\n   414→\t}\n   415→\treturn false\n   416→}\n   417→\n   418→// getToken retrieves a new accessToken and stores the newly retrieved token in the tokenProvider.\n   419→func (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) getToken(ctx context.Context) error {\n   420→\taccessToken, err := tokenProvider.credentialClient.GetToken(ctx, *tokenProvider.options)\n   421→\tif err != nil {\n   422→\t\treturn err\n   423→\t}\n   424→\tif len(accessToken.Token) == 0 {\n   425→\t\treturn errors.New(\"access token is empty\")\n   426→\t}\n   427→\n   428→\ttokenProvider.token = accessToken.Token\n   429→\terr = tokenProvider.updateRefreshTime(accessToken)\n   430→\tif err != nil {\n   431→\t\treturn err\n   432→\t}\n   433→\treturn nil\n   434→}\n   435→\n   436→// updateRefreshTime handles logic to set refreshTime. The refreshTime is set at half the duration of the actual token expiry.\n   437→func (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) updateRefreshTime(accessToken azcore.AccessToken) error {\n   438→\ttokenExpiryTimestamp := accessToken.ExpiresOn.UTC()\n   439→\tdeltaExpirytime := time.Now().Add(time.Until(tokenExpiryTimestamp) / 2)\n   440→\tif !deltaExpirytime.After(time.Now().UTC()) {\n   441→\t\treturn errors.New(\"access token expiry is less than the current time\")\n   442→\t}\n   443→\ttokenProvider.refreshTime = deltaExpirytime\n   444→\treturn nil\n   445→}\n   446→\n   447→// getAudience returns audiences for different clouds.\n   448→func getAudience(cloud string) (string, error) {\n   449→\tswitch strings.ToLower(cloud) {\n   450→\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureChina):\n   451→\t\treturn IngestionChinaAudience, nil\n   452→\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureGovernment):\n   453→\t\treturn IngestionGovernmentAudience, nil\n   454→\tcase strings.ToLower(AzurePublic):\n   455→\t\treturn IngestionPublicAudience, nil\n   456→\tdefault:\n   457→\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Cloud is not specified or is incorrect: \" + cloud)\n   458→\t}\n   459→}\n   460→\n   461→// getCloudConfiguration returns the cloud Configuration which contains AAD endpoint for different clouds.\n   462→func getCloudConfiguration(c string) (cloud.Configuration, error) {\n   463→\tswitch strings.ToLower(c) {\n   464→\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureChina):\n   465→\t\treturn cloud.AzureChina, nil\n   466→\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureGovernment):\n   467→\t\treturn cloud.AzureGovernment, nil\n   468→\tcase strings.ToLower(AzurePublic):\n   469→\t\treturn cloud.AzurePublic, nil\n   470→\tdefault:\n   471→\t\treturn cloud.Configuration{}, errors.New(\"Cloud is not specified or is incorrect: \" + c)\n   472→\t}\n   473→}\n   474→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. error {\n\ttype plain AzureADConfig\n\t*c = AzureADConfig{}\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\treturn c.Validate()\n}\n\n// NewAzureADRoundTripper creates round tripper adding Azure AD authorization to calls.\nfunc NewAzureADRoundTripper(cfg *AzureADConfig, next http.RoundTripper) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\tif next == nil {\n\t\tnext = http.DefaultTransport\n\t}\n\n\tcred, err := newTokenCredential(cfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttokenProvider, err := newTokenProvider(cfg, cred)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\trt := &azureADRoundTripper{\n\t\tnext:          next,\n\t\ttokenProvider: tokenProvider,\n\t}\n\treturn rt, nil\n}\n\n// RoundTrip sets Authorization header for requests.\nfunc (rt *azureADRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\taccessToken, err := rt.tokenProvider.getAccessToken(req.Context())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tbearerAccessToken := \"Bearer \" + accessToken\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", bearerAccessToken)\n\n\treturn rt.next.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\n// newTokenCredential returns a cloudConfiguration,\n\t}\n\n\tif cfg.ManagedIdentity != nil {\n\t\tmanagedIdentityConfig := &ManagedIdentityConfig{\n\t\t\tClientID: cfg.ManagedIdentity.ClientID,\n\t\t}\n\t\tcred, err = This accessToken is attached to the Authorization header while making requests.\nfunc newTokenProvider(cfg *AzureADConfig, cred azcore.TokenCredential) (*tokenProvider, error) {\n\tvar scopes []string\n\n\t// Use custom scope if provided, otherwise fallback to cloud-specific audience\n\tif cfg.Scope != \"\" {\n\t\tscopes = []string{cfg.Scope}\n\t} else {\n\t\taudience, err := in the token provider is valid and not expired.\nfunc (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) valid() bool {\n\tif len(tokenProvider.token) == 0 {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tif tokenProvider.refreshTime.After(time.Now().UTC()) {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// getToken retrieves a new accessToken and stores the newly retrieved token in the tokenProvider.\nfunc (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) getToken(ctx context.Context) error {\n\taccessToken, err := tokenProvider.credentialClient.GetToken(ctx, *tokenProvider.options)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn tokenProvider.updateRefreshTime(accessToken)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// updateRefreshTime handles logic to set refreshTime. The refreshTime is set at half the duration of the actual token expiry.\nfunc (tokenProvider *tokenProvider) updateRefreshTime(accessToken azcore.AccessToken) error {\n\ttokenExpiryTimestamp := accessToken.ExpiresOn.UTC()\n\tdeltaExpirytime := time.Now().Add(time.Until(tokenExpiryTimestamp) / 2)\n\tif !deltaExpirytime.After(time.Now().UTC()) {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"access token expiry is less than the current time\")\n\t}\n\ttokenProvider.refreshTime = deltaExpirytime\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// getAudience returns audiences for different clouds.\nfunc getAudience(cloud string) (string, error) {\n\tswitch strings.ToLower(cloud) {\n\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureChina):\n\t\treturn IngestionChinaAudience, nil\n\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureGovernment):\n\t\treturn IngestionGovernmentAudience, nil\n\tcase strings.ToLower(AzurePublic):\n\t\treturn IngestionPublicAudience, nil\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"Cloud is not specified or is incorrect: \" + cloud)\n\t}\n}\n\n// getCloudConfiguration returns the cloud Configuration which contains AAD endpoint for different clouds.\nfunc getCloudConfiguration(c string) (cloud.Configuration, error) {\n\tswitch strings.ToLower(c) {\n\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureChina):\n\t\treturn cloud.AzureChina, nil\n\tcase strings.ToLower(AzureGovernment):\n\t\treturn cloud.AzureGovernment, nil\n\tcase strings.ToLower(AzurePublic):\n\t\treturn cloud.AzurePublic, nil\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn cloud.Configuration{}, errors.New(\"Cloud is not specified or is incorrect: \" + c)\n\t}\n}\n","numLines":474,"startLine":1,"totalLines":474}}}
